 sachiv ajay shirke ne samiti se nirdesh maange the ki kya unhen isibi se apane bhugtan karne ke liye bol dena chahie kyonki bisisiai vittiya lenden nahin kar saktaa kyonki dwipaksheeya siries ke dauraan daura karne vaali team ke liye bhugtan or saare intjamaat gharelu board dwaara hi kiye jate hai
 In response, the Lodha panel said, 'the proposed mou between BCCI and ECB pertains to bilateral cricket policy which is not an essential part of the committee's order
 jahaan tak bhugtan kaa sambandh he, agar ye bisisiai dwaara sidhe diye jate hai to is samiti dwaara tab tak koi nirdesh nahin diye ja sakate hai, jab tak bisisiai dwaara maamle se sambandhit jaankaree muhaiyaa nahin karaayi jaati
 In an email written by panel secretary Gopal Shankaranarayana said, "in order to avoid any obstruction in the cricket calendar and to ensure that the lovers of the game are entertained, the BCCI is advised to submit to the Supreme Court on 18 July 2016, Follow the instructions given in the order of 7 October 2016 and 21 October 2016

 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Punjab National Bank (PNB) customers will have to pay for ATM transactions more than 5 times a month
 yah niyam oktober maheene se lagu hoga
 At present, customers do not have to pay any fees for any financial and non-financial transactions done through PNB atms in a month
 haalanki nayaa niyam lagu hone ke baad se yah suvidha samaapt ho jaaegi
 Punjab National Bank stated in the notice issued to the customers, “the number of free transactions for PNB customers from PNB atms and charges on transactions exceeding free transactions have been revised
 1 oktober 2017 se sanshodhit shulk lagu honge
 The bank said that Savings / Current / Overdraft account holders will be charged Rs 10 per transaction for more than five times a month
 bhale hi pienbi card dharak keval pienbi atm par hi lenden kare
 Thus, customers will have to pay a fee for exceeding the free limit financial transactions (withdrawing money from atms) and non-financial transactions (withdrawing mini statements)
